)@@G@@                    . END OF DOCUMENTATION@E@@@#          GO ENDDOC     FR
)@@G@@              . BYPASS DOCUMENTATION@G@@@#          'THIS FUNCTION DUMPSFS
)@@G@@ AN AREA OF MEMORY AS ASCII CHARACTERS.'  @B@@@#          'FORMAT:  ADUMFT
)@@G@@P (START, LENGTH)'@G@@@#          'WHERE ''START'' IS THE STARTING ADDREFU
)@@G@@SS, AND ''LENGTH'' IS'  @B@@@#          'THE NUMBER OF WORDS TO DUMP.'  FV
)@@G@@@F@@@#          'FOR ADDITIONAL INFORMATION, CALL  LCLAIDS (''DUMP'') .'FW
)@@G@@@E@@@#ENDDOC:                               . END OF DOCUMENTATION@G@@@@FX
)@@G@@          LOCAL N,REL,WORDS,LEFT,FILE,DIF,SKIP,L1,L2,L3,L4,P1,P2,P3,P4  FY
)@@G@@@^@@@@          LOCAL DUMP(5) @F@@@@          GO (START++LENGTH++OFFSET=FZ
)@@G@@/0)++(DUMP[1,,$H2]=/'DMP')++; @E@@@@               (DUMP[0]=/DUMP[2]+DUMGA
)@@G@@P[3]+DUMP[4])\NEWDUMP   @G@@@@          START:=DUMP[2]-DUMP[3]*(DUMP[1,,GB
)@@G@@$H1]=/'**A')*(1-2*(DUMP[2]<0))@ @@@@          LENGTH:=DUMP[3]     @E@@@@GC
)@@G@@          OFFSET:=DUMP[4]-DUMP[3]*(DUMP[1,,$H1]=/'**A')     @ @@@@NEWDUMGD
)@@G@@P:  DUMP[1]:='**ADMP'   @F@@@@          LENGTH:=LENGTH+(LENGTH=0)   . DUGE
)@@G@@MP AT LEAST ONE WORD    @H@@@@          GO START>=0\RELDUMP         . ISGF
)@@G@@ THIS AN ABSOLUTE DUMP REQUEST?     @C@@@@          START:=-START       GG
)@@G@@        . YES     @#@@@@          P3:=[*] @#@@@@          P4:=[*] @A@@@@GH
)@@G@@RELDUMP:  DUMP[2]:=START+LENGTH     @ @@@@          DUMP[3]:=LENGTH     GI
)@@G@@@A@@@@          DUMP[4]:=OFFSET+LENGTH    @B@@@@          DUMP[0]:=DUMP[GJ
)@@G@@2]+DUMP[3]+DUMP[4]@F@@@@          GO START<28*/24\NOFILE      . IS THIS GK
)@@G@@A FILE<N> SPEC?   @E@@@@          FILE:=START*/-24/28         . COMPUTE GL
)@@G@@FILE NUMBER @G@@@@          'DUMPING FROM FILE',FILE[,,$U!D],0[,,$U!SKIPGM
)@@G@@],', TRACK',;     @D@@@@               ((START-FILE*28*/24)/1792)[,,$U!DGN
)@@G@@]     @E@@@@          DIF:=(START-FILE*28*/24)/1792*1792+FILE*28*/24    GO
)@@G@@@I@@@@. ----------------------------------------------------------------GP
)@@G@@--------------    @F@@@@NOFILE:   L1:=6+2*(START-DIF>0777777) . LENGTH OGQ
)@@G@@F LEADING ADDRESS @I@@@@          L2:=3+(LENGTH+OFFSET>1*/9)+2*(LENGTH+OGR
)@@G@@FFSET>1*/12) . LENGTH OF REL ADD    @F@@@@          L3:=12              GS
)@@G@@        . LENGTH OF FIRST DATA FIELD@G@@@@          L4:=4               GT
)@@G@@        . LENGTH OF SECOND DATA FIELD     @H@@@@          P1:=[,,$U!O]++GU
)@@G@@L1*/18        . EDITING FORMAT FOR LEADING ADDRESS    @H@@@@          P2GV
)@@G@@:=[,,$U!O]++L2*/18        . EDITING FORMAT FOR RELATIVE ADDRESS   @F@@@@GW
)@@G@@          P3:=[!O]++L3*/18++P3        . FIRST DATA EDITING FORMAT @F@@@@GX
)@@G@@          P4:=[!A]++L4*/18++P4        . SECOND DATA EDITING FORMAT@I@@@@GY
)@@G@@. ----------------------------------------------------------------------GZ
)@@G@@--------    @F@@@@          LENGTH:=LENGTH+(LENGTH=0)   . DUMP AT LEAST HA
)@@G@@ONE WORD    @H@@@@          N:=($LINSIZ-L1-L2-2)/(L3+L4+2) . COMPUTE NUMHB
)@@G@@BER OF WORDS PER LINE   @F@@@@          GO LENGTH<1\0,N<9\$+2       . VAHC
)@@G@@LID WORDS PER LINE?     @F@@@@          N:=8                        . MAHD
)@@G@@XIMUM OF 8 WORDS/LINE   @G@@@@          GO N>0\$+2                  . ATHE
)@@G@@ LEAST ONE WORD PER LINE?     @#@@@@          N:=1    @F@@@@          WOHF
)@@G@@RDS:=N                    . WORDS ON CURRENT LINE     @I@@@@          LEHG
)@@G@@FT:=$LINSIZ-N*(L3+L4+2)-L1-L2-2=/0 . ONE IF LINE HAS LEFTOVER SPACES    HH
)@@G@@@E@@@@LINE:     GO LENGTH-REL>=WORDS\CHECK  . SHORT LAST LINE?    @F@@@@HI
)@@G@@          WORDS:=LENGTH-REL           . WORDS TO EDIT ON LAST LINE@G@@@@HJ
)@@G@@          GO REL\DOIT                 . IS THIS ALSO THE FIRST LINE?    HK
)@@G@@@G@@@@          LEFT:=1                     . THERE IS DEFINATELY ROOM LHL
)@@G@@EFT   @F@@@@          N:=WORDS                    . YES -- EDIT A SHORT HM
)@@G@@LINE  @G@@@@CHECK:    GO (REL=0)++(WORDS=LENGTH-REL)\DOIT . FIRST OR LASHN
)@@G@@T LINE?     @I@@@@          GO START[REL:WORDS]=START[REL-WORDS:WORDS]\SHO
)@@G@@KIPIT . SAME AS LAST LINE?    @I@@@@DOIT:     (START-DIF)[REL++P1],(REL+HP
)@@G@@OFFSET)[P2],LEFT--SKIP\0[2*LEFT,,$U!SKIP],;     @D@@@@          SKIP\('*HQ
)@@G@@',0[,,$U!SKIP]),START[REL++P3],;    @F@@@@          WORDS>1\START[REL+1+HR
)@@G@@+P3],WORDS>2\START[REL+2++P3],;     @F@@@@          WORDS>3\START[REL+3+HS
)@@G@@+P3],WORDS>4\START[REL+4++P3],;     @F@@@@          WORDS>5\START[REL+5+HT
)@@G@@+P3],WORDS>6\START[REL+6++P3],;     @G@@@@          WORDS>7\START[REL+7+HU
)@@G@@+P3],(L1+L2+LEFT+L3*N+N)[4,,$U!TAB],;     @D@@@@          START[REL++P4]HV
)@@G@@,WORDS>1\START[REL+1++P4],;   @F@@@@          WORDS>2\START[REL+2++P4],WHW
)@@G@@ORDS>3\START[REL+3++P4],;     @F@@@@          WORDS>4\START[REL+4++P4],WHX
)@@G@@ORDS>5\START[REL+5++P4],;     @E@@@@          WORDS>6\START[REL+6++P4],WHY
)@@G@@ORDS>7\START[REL+7++P4] @E@@@@          SKIP:=0                     . CLHZ
)@@G@@EAR SKIPPING FLAG @#@@@@          GO $+2  @E@@@@SKIPIT:   SKIP:=1       IA
)@@G@@              . SET SKIPPING FLAG   @F@@@@          REL:=REL+WORDS      IB
)@@G@@        . ADVANCE RELATIVE POINTER  @C@@@@          GO REL<LENGTH\LINE  IC
)@@G@@        . LOOP    @[@@@@END   ___ CHARACTERS.'  @[@@@8@ @@@9@H@@@"@C@@[FID
)@@G@@@G@@[N@C@@[Z@G@@[$@4@@[3@%@@]$@D@@#L@U@@#U@D@@#4@D@@#.@E@@^A@ @@^K@B@@^PIE

)@@G@@WORDS STARTING AT <START>     @I@@@@                                    UK
)@@G@@  . USE <OFFSET> AS LOWEST RELATIVE ADDRESS     @E@@@]          GO ENDDOUL
)@@G@@C                   . BYPASS DOCUMENTATION@H@@@]          'THIS FUNCTIONUM
)@@G@@ DUMPS AN AREA OF MEMORY AS FIELDATA CHARACTERS.'     @B@@@]          'FUN
)@@G@@ORMAT:  FDUMP (START, LENGTH)'@G@@@]          'WHERE ''START'' IS THE STUO
)@@G@@ARTING ADDRESS, AND ''LENGTH'' IS'  @B@@@]          'THE NUMBER OF WORDSUP
)@@G@@ TO DUMP.'  @F@@@]          'FOR ADDITIONAL INFORMATION, CALL  LCLAIDS (UQ
)@@G@@''DUMP'') .'@E@@@]ENDDOC:                               . END OF DOCUMENUR

)@@G@@@H@]@[          'THIS FUNCTION DUMPS AN AREA OF MEMORY AS FIELDATA CHARAUT
)@@G@@CTERS.'     @B@]@[          'FORMAT:  FDUMP (START, LENGTH)'@G@]@[      UU
)@@G@@    'WHERE ''START''' IS THE STARTING ADDRESS, AND ''LENGTH'' IS' @B@]@[UV
)@@G@@          'THE NUMBER OF WORDS TO DUMP.'  @F@]@[          'FOR ADDITIONAUW
)@@G@@L INFORMATION, CALL  LCLAIDS ('DUMP') .'  @E@]@[ENDDOC:                 UX
)@@G@@              . END OF DOCUMENTATION@G@@@@          LOCAL N,REL,WORDS,LEUY
)@@G@@FT,FILE,DIF,SKIP,L1,L2,L3,L4,P1,P2,P3,P4  @^@@@@          LOCAL DUMP(5) UZ
)@@G@@@F@@@@          GO (START++LENGTH++OFFSET=/0)++(DUMP[1,,$H2]=/'DMP')++; VA
)@@G@@@E@@@@               (DUMP[0]=/DUMP[2]+DUMP[3]+DUMP[4])\NEWDUMP   @G@@@@VB
)@@G@@          START:=DUMP[2]-DUMP[3]*(DUMP[1,,$H1]=/'**F')*(1-2*(DUMP[2]<0))VC
)@@G@@@ @@@@          LENGTH:=DUMP[3]     @E@@@@          OFFSET:=DUMP[4]-DUMPVD
)@@G@@[3]*(DUMP[1,,$H1]=/'**F')     @ @@@@NEWDUMP:  DUMP[1]:='**FDMP'   @F@@@@VE
)@@G@@          LENGTH:=LENGTH+(LENGTH=0)   . DUMP AT LEAST ONE WORD    @H@@@@VF
)@@G@@          GO START>=0\RELDUMP         . IS THIS AN ABSOLUTE DUMP REQUESTVG
)@@G@@?     @C@@@@          START:=-START               . YES     @#@@@@      VH
)@@G@@    P3:=[*] @#@@@@          P4:=[*] @A@@@@RELDUMP:  DUMP[2]:=START+LENGTVI
)@@G@@H     @ @@@@          DUMP[3]:=LENGTH     @A@@@@          DUMP[4]:=OFFSEVJ
)@@G@@T+LENGTH    @B@@@@          DUMP[0]:=DUMP[2]+DUMP[3]+DUMP[4]@F@@@@      VK
)@@G@@    GO START<28*/24\NOFILE      . IS THIS A FILE<N> SPEC?   @E@@@@      VL
)@@G@@    FILE:=START*/-24/28         . COMPUTE FILE NUMBER @G@@@@          'DVM
)@@G@@UMPING FROM FILE',FILE[,,$U!D],0[,,$U!SKIP],', TRACK',;     @D@@@@      VN
)@@G@@         ((START-FILE*28*/24)/1792)[,,$U!D]     @E@@@@          DIF:=(STVO
)@@G@@ART-FILE*28*/24)/1792*1792+FILE*28*/24    @I@@@@. ----------------------VP
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------    @F@@@@NOFILEVQ
)@@G@@:   L1:=6+2*(START-DIF>0777777) . LENGTH OF LEADING ADDRESS @I@@@@      VR
)@@G@@    L2:=3+(LENGTH+OFFSET>1*/9)+2*(LENGTH+OFFSET>1*/12) . LENGTH OF REL AVS
)@@G@@DD    @F@@@@          L3:=12                      . LENGTH OF FIRST DATAVT
)@@G@@ FIELD@G@@@@          L4:=6                       . LENGTH OF SECOND DATVU
)@@G@@A FIELD     @H@@@@          P1:=[,,$U!O]++L1*/18        . EDITING FORMATVV
)@@G@@ FOR LEADING ADDRESS    @H@@@@          P2:=[,,$U!O]++L2*/18        . EDVW
)@@G@@ITING FORMAT FOR RELATIVE ADDRESS   @F@@@@          P3:=[!O]++L3*/18++P3VX
)@@G@@        . FIRST DATA EDITING FORMAT @F@@@@          P4:=[!F]++L4*/18++P4VY
)@@G@@        . SECOND DATA EDITING FORMAT@I@@@@. ----------------------------VZ
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------    @F@@@@          LEWA
)@@G@@NGTH:=LENGTH+(LENGTH=0)   . DUMP AT LEAST ONE WORD    @H@@@@          N:WB
)@@G@@=($LINSIZ-L1-L2-2)/(L3+L4+2) . COMPUTE NUMBER OF WORDS PER LINE   @F@@@@WC
)@@G@@          GO LENGTH<1\0,N<9\$+2       . VALID WORDS PER LINE?     @F@@@@WD
)@@G@@          N:=8                        . MAXIMUM OF 8 WORDS/LINE   @G@@@@WE
)@@G@@          GO N>0\$+2                  . AT LEAST ONE WORD PER LINE?     WF
)@@G@@@#@@@@          N:=1    @F@@@@          WORDS:=N                    . WOWG
)@@G@@RDS ON CURRENT LINE     @I@@@@          LEFT:=$LINSIZ-N*(L3+L4+2)-L1-L2-WH
)@@G@@2=/0 . ONE IF LINE HAS LEFTOVER SPACES    @E@@@@LINE:     GO LENGTH-REL>WI
)@@G@@=WORDS\CHECK  . SHORT LAST LINE?    @F@@@@          WORDS:=LENGTH-REL   WJ
)@@G@@        . WORDS TO EDIT ON LAST LINE@G@@@@          GO REL\DOIT         WK
)@@G@@        . IS THIS ALSO THE FIRST LINE?    @G@@@@          LEFT:=1       WL
)@@G@@              . THERE IS DEFINATELY ROOM LEFT   @F@@@@          N:=WORDSWM
)@@G@@                    . YES -- EDIT A SHORT LINE  @G@@@@CHECK:    GO (REL=WN
)@@G@@0)++(WORDS=LENGTH-REL)\DOIT . FIRST OR LAST LINE?     @I@@@@          GOWO
)@@G@@ START[REL:WORDS]=START[REL-WORDS:WORDS]\SKIPIT . SAME AS LAST LINE?    WP
)@@G@@@I@@@@DOIT:     (START-DIF)[REL++P1],(REL+OFFSET)[P2],LEFT--SKIP\0[2*LEFWQ
)@@G@@T,,$U!SKIP],;     @D@@@@          SKIP\('*',0[,,$U!SKIP]),START[REL++P3]WR
)@@G@@,;    @F@@@@          WORDS>1\START[REL+1++P3],WORDS>2\START[REL+2++P3],WS

)@@G@@    GO $+2  @E@@@@SKIPIT:   SKIP:=1                     . SET SKIPPING FXB

)@@G@@[[#__;^@[BTD@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@[[#__$]@[@@@@@@@@A[@^@@@[[#_";[@K@@@[@N@@@PW

)@@G@@@@@@@@[[#__$[[#__$[[#__<[@^@@@[@\@@@@@@@@@[[#__$[[#__7[@E@@@[@Q@@][[#_"$QA
)@@G@@[@X@@@@@@@@@[@4@@@@@@@@@^@ @@@@@@@@ @KIPIT      ^@ @@@@@@@@0SKIPIT      QB
)@@G@@^@ @@@@@@@@!DOIT        ^@ @@@@@@@@:CHECK       ^@ @@@@@@@@&LINE        QC
)@@G@@^@ @@@@@@@@SNOFILE      ^@ @@@@@@@@KRELDUMP     ^@ @@@@@@@@FNEWDUMP     QD
)@@G@@^[ @@@@@@@@@DUMP        ^@ @@@@@@@@@P3          ^@ @@@@@@@@@P2          QE
)@@G@@^@ @@@@@@@@@P1          ^@ @@@@@@@@@L3          ^@ @@@@@@@@@L2          QF
)@@G@@^@ @@@@@@@@@L1          ^@ @@@@@@@@@SKIP        ^@ @@@@@@@@@DIF         QG
)@@G@@^@ @@@@@@@@@FILE        ^@ @@@@@@@@@LEFT        ^@ @@@@@@@@@WORDS       QH
)@@G@@^@ @@@@@@@@@REL         ^@ @@@@@@@@@N           ^@ @@@@@@@@BENDDOC      QI
)@@G@@^@ @@@@@@@@XOFFSET      ^@ @@@@@@@@WLENGTH      ^@ @@@@@@@@TSTART       QJ
)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@I@@@@FUNCT QEDUMP(START,LENGTH,OFFSET)     . DUMP <LENGTH> QK
)@@G@@WORDS STARTING AT <START>     @I@@@@                                    QL
)@@G@@  . USE <OFFSET> AS LOWEST RELATIVE ADDRESS     @E@]@[          GO ENDDOQM
)@@G@@C                   . BYPASS DOCUMENTATION@H@]@[ 'THIS FUNCTION DUMPS ANQN
)@@G@@ AREA OF MEMORY AS EBCDIC CHARACTERS AND IN HEX.'     @C@]@[          'FQO
)@@G@@ORMAT:  QEDUMP (START, LENGTH)'     @G@]@[          'WHERE ''START''' ISQP
)@@G@@ THE STARTING ADDRESS, AND ''LENGTH'' IS' @B@]@[          'THE NUMBER OFQQ
)@@G@@ WORDS TO DUMP.'  @F@]@[          'FOR ADDITIONAL INFORMATION, CALL  LCLQR
)@@G@@AIDS ('DUMP') .'  @E@]@[ENDDOC:                               . END OF DQS
)@@G@@OCUMENTATION@E@@@]          GO ENDDOC                   . BYPASS DOCUMENQT
)@@G@@TATION@H@@@]  'THIS FUNCTION DUMPS AN AREA OF MEMORY AS EBCDIC CHARACTERQU
)@@G@@S AND IN HEX.'    @C@@@]          'FORMAT:  QEDUMP (START, LENGTH)'     QV
)@@G@@@G@@@]          'WHERE ''START'' IS THE STARTING ADDRESS, AND ''LENGTH''QW
)@@G@@ IS'  @B@@@]          'THE NUMBER OF WORDS TO DUMP.'  @F@@@]          'FQX
)@@G@@OR ADDITIONAL INFORMATION, CALL  LCLAIDS (''DUMP'') .'@E@@@]ENDDOC:     QY
)@@G@@                          . END OF DOCUMENTATION@G@@@@          LOCAL N,QZ
)@@G@@REL,WORDS,LEFT,FILE,DIF,SKIP,L1,L2,L3,L4,P1,P2,P3,P4  @^@@@@          LORA
)@@G@@CAL DUMP(5) @F@@@@          GO (START++LENGTH++OFFSET=/0)++(DUMP[1,,$H2]RB
)@@G@@=/'DMP')++; @E@@@@               (DUMP[0]=/DUMP[2]+DUMP[3]+DUMP[4])\NEWDRC
)@@G@@UMP   @G@@@@          START:=DUMP[2]-DUMP[3]*(DUMP[1,,$H1]=/'*QE')*(1-2*RD
)@@G@@(DUMP[2]<0))@ @@@@          LENGTH:=DUMP[3]     @E@@@@          OFFSET:=RE
)@@G@@DUMP[4]-DUMP[3]*(DUMP[1,,$H1]=/'*QE')     @ @@@@NEWDUMP:  DUMP[1]:='*QEDRF
)@@G@@MP'   @F@@@@          LENGTH:=LENGTH+(LENGTH=0)   . DUMP AT LEAST ONE WORG
)@@G@@RD    @H@@@@          GO START>=0\RELDUMP         . IS THIS AN ABSOLUTE RH
)@@G@@DUMP REQUEST?     @C@@@@          START:=-START               . YES     RI
)@@G@@@#@@@@          P3:=[*] @#@@@@          P4:=[*] @A@@@@RELDUMP:  DUMP[2]:RJ
)@@G@@=START+LENGTH     @ @@@@          DUMP[3]:=LENGTH     @A@@@@          DURK
)@@G@@MP[4]:=OFFSET+LENGTH    @B@@@@          DUMP[0]:=DUMP[2]+DUMP[3]+DUMP[4]RL
)@@G@@@F@@@@          GO START<28*/24\NOFILE      . IS THIS A FILE<N> SPEC?   RM
)@@G@@@E@@@@          FILE:=START*/-24/28         . COMPUTE FILE NUMBER @G@@@@RN
)@@G@@          'DUMPING FROM FILE',FILE[,,$U!D],0[,,$U!SKIP],', TRACK',;     RO
)@@G@@@D@@@@               ((START-FILE*28*/24)/1792)[,,$U!D]     @E@@@@      RP
)@@G@@    DIF:=(START-FILE*28*/24)/1792*1792+FILE*28*/24    @I@@@@. ----------RQ
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------------    RR
)@@G@@@F@@@@NOFILE:   L1:=4+2*(START-DIF>0177777) . LENGTH OF LEADING ADDRESS RS
)@@G@@@I@@@@          L2:=2+(LENGTH+OFFSET>1*/8)+2*(LENGTH+OFFSET>1*/12) . LENRT
)@@G@@GTH OF REL ADD    @F@@@@          L3:=8                       . LENGTH ORU
)@@G@@F FIRST DATA FIELD@G@@@@          L4:=4                       . LENGTH ORV
)@@G@@F SECOND DATA FIELD     @H@@@@          P1:=[,,$U!H]++L1*/18        . EDRW
)@@G@@ITING FORMAT FOR LEADING ADDRESS    @H@@@@          P2:=[,,$U!H]++L2*/18RX
)@@G@@        . EDITING FORMAT FOR RELATIVE ADDRESS   @F@@@@          P3:=[!QHRY
)@@G@@]++L3*/18++P3       . FIRST DATA EDITING FORMAT @F@@@@          P4:=[!QERZ
)@@G@@]++L4*/18++P4       . SECOND DATA EDITING FORMAT@I@@@@. ----------------SA
)@@G@@--------------------------------------------------------------    @F@@@@SB
)@@G@@          LENGTH:=LENGTH+(LENGTH=0)   . DUMP AT LEAST ONE WORD    @H@@@@SC
)@@G@@          N:=($LINSIZ-L1-L2-2)/(L3+L4+2) . COMPUTE NUMBER OF WORDS PER LSD
)@@G@@INE   @F@@@@          GO LENGTH<1\0,N<9\$+2       . VALID WORDS PER LINESE
)@@G@@?     @F@@@@          N:=8                        . MAXIMUM OF 8 WORDS/LSF
)@@G@@INE   @G@@@@          GO N>0\$+2                  . AT LEAST ONE WORD PESG
)@@G@@R LINE?     @#@@@@          N:=1    @F@@@@          WORDS:=N            SH
)@@G@@        . WORDS ON CURRENT LINE     @I@@@@          LEFT:=$LINSIZ-N*(L3+SI
)@@G@@L4+2)-L1-L2-2=/0 . ONE IF LINE HAS LEFTOVER SPACES    @E@@@@LINE:     GOSJ
)@@G@@ LENGTH-REL>=WORDS\CHECK  . SHORT LAST LINE?    @F@@@@          WORDS:=LSK
)@@G@@ENGTH-REL           . WORDS TO EDIT ON LAST LINE@G@@@@          GO REL\DSL
)@@G@@OIT                 . IS THIS ALSO THE FIRST LINE?    @G@@@@          LESM
)@@G@@FT:=1                     . THERE IS DEFINATELY ROOM LEFT   @F@@@@      SN
)@@G@@    N:=WORDS                    . YES -- EDIT A SHORT LINE  @G@@@@CHECK:SO
)@@G@@    GO (REL=0)++(WORDS=LENGTH-REL)\DOIT . FIRST OR LAST LINE?     @I@@@@SP
)@@G@@          GO START[REL:WORDS]=START[REL-WORDS:WORDS]\SKIPIT . SAME AS LASQ
)@@G@@ST LINE?    @I@@@@DOIT:     (START-DIF)[REL++P1],(REL+OFFSET)[P2],LEFT--SR
)@@G@@SKIP\0[2*LEFT,,$U!SKIP],;     @D@@@@          SKIP\('*',0[,,$U!SKIP]),STSS
)@@G@@ART[REL++P3],;    @F@@@@          WORDS>1\START[REL+1++P3],WORDS>2\STARTST
)@@G@@[REL+2++P3],;     @F@@@@          WORDS>3\START[REL+3++P3],WORDS>4\STARTSU
)@@G@@[REL+4++P3],;     @F@@@@          WORDS>5\START[REL+5++P3],WORDS>6\STARTSV
)@@G@@[REL+6++P3],;     @G@@@@          WORDS>7\START[REL+7++P3],(L1+L2+LEFT+LSW
)@@G@@3*N+N)[4,,$U!TAB],;     @D@@@@          START[REL++P4],WORDS>1\START[RELSX
)@@G@@+1++P4],;   @F@@@@          WORDS>2\START[REL+2++P4],WORDS>3\START[REL+3SY
)@@G@@++P4],;     @F@@@@          WORDS>4\START[REL+4++P4],WORDS>5\START[REL+5SZ
)@@G@@++P4],;     @E@@@@          WORDS>6\START[REL+6++P4],WORDS>7\START[REL+7TA
)@@G@@++P4] @E@@@@          SKIP:=0                     . CLEAR SKIPPING FLAG TB
)@@G@@@#@@@@          GO $+2  @E@@@@SKIPIT:   SKIP:=1                     . SETC
)@@G@@T SKIPPING FLAG   @F@@@@          REL:=REL+WORDS              . ADVANCE TD
)@@G@@RELATIVE POINTER  @C@@@@          GO REL<LENGTH\LINE          . LOOP    TE
)@@G@@@[@@@@END   ___@@[A#)^<)=8)@@]A:)^[XC'0@@[=8)@@^]]0^FK>8)@@C[]0^<->8)@@KTF
